29  package sun.nio.cs.ext;
30  
31  import java.nio.charset.Charset;
32  import java.nio.charset.CharsetEncoder;
33  
34  public class JIS_X_0208_Encoder extends DoubleByteEncoder
35  {
36  
37      /*
38       * default replacement defined merely for pseudo
39       * charset x-JIS-X-0208 to instantiate with a
40       * decodeable replacement byte sequence
41       * JIS X 0208(1987) 0x2129 maps to FULLWIDTH QUESTION MARK
42       *
43       */
44  
45      private static byte[] repl = { (byte)0x21, (byte)0x29 };
46  
47      public JIS_X_0208_Encoder(Charset cs) {
48          super(cs,
49                index1,
50                index2 ,
51                repl
52               );
53      }
54      public JIS_X_0208_Encoder(Charset cs, float avg, float max) {
55          super(cs,
56                index1,
57                index2 ,
58                repl,
59                avg,
60                max
61               );
62      }
63  
64      protected int encodeSingle(char inputChar) {
65          return -1;
66      }
67  
68      /**
69       * These accessors are temporarily supplied while sun.io
70       * converters co-exist with the sun.nio.cs.{ext} charset coders
71       * These facilitate sharing of conversion tables between the
72       * two co-existing implementations. When sun.io converters
73       * are made extinct these will be unncessary and should be removed
74       */
75  
76      public static short[] getIndex1() {
77         return index1;
78      }
79  
80      public static String[] getIndex2() {
81         return index2;
82      }
